            color: white;

<script type="text/javascript">

        var idPass = $('#id_password');
        var abccc = true

        function disabledPassShowOption() {
            var passwordVal_length = idPass.val().length;
            console.log('passwordVal_length', passwordVal_length);
            if(abccc) {
                if(passwordVal_length) {
                    $('.password-show-hide').hide();
                }else {
                    $('.password-show-hide').show();
                    abccc = false
                }
            }
        }
        idPass.on('keyup', function(){
            disabledPassShowOption();
        })


        $('.password-show-hide').on('click', function(){
            var $this= $(this),
                $passwordField = $this.parent().find('input');
            
            // Changing input type
            if( $passwordField.attr('type') == "password" ) {
                $passwordField.attr('type', 'text');
            }else {
                $passwordField.attr('type', 'password');
            }

            // Changing Icon
            if( $this.find('i').hasClass('eye') ) {
                $this.find('i').removeClass('eye').addClass('hide');
            }else {
                $this.find('i').removeClass('hide').addClass('eye');
            }
        });
</script>
            </div>

            /* Wizard Script */
            // Variables
            var $nextStep = $('.next-step'),
                $nextStepName = $('.next-step-name'),
                $nextStepNumber = $('.next-step-number'),
                $currentStep = $('.current-step'),
                $currentStepName = $('.current-step-name'),
                $currentStepNumber = $('.current-step-number'),
                $prevStep = $('.prev-step'),
                $prevStepName = $('.prev-step-name'),
                $prevStepNumber = $('.prev-step-number');

            $nextStepName.text( returnStepName(2) );
            $prevStepName.text( returnStepName(1) );

            $nextStep.on('click', function(e) {
                var count = Number( $nextStep.attr('data-step') );
                if ( count != '8' ) {
                    $nextStepName.text( returnStepName(count) );
                    $prevStepName.text( returnStepName(count-1) );
                }
                $nextStep.popup('hide');
                oldWizard(count-1, 'next');
            });

            $nextStep.hover(function(e) {
                var count = Number( $nextStep.attr('data-step') );
                if ( count != '8' ) {
                    $nextStep.attr('data-content', returnStepName(count) );
                }
            });

            $prevStep.on('click', function(e) {
                var count = Number( $prevStep.attr('data-step') );
                $nextStepName.text( returnStepName(count+1) );
                $prevStepName.text( returnStepName(count) );
                $prevStep.popup('hide');
                stepChanges('previous');
            });

            $prevStep.hover(function(e) {
                var count = Number( $prevStep.attr('data-step') );
                $prevStep.attr('data-content', returnStepName(count) );
            });

            function stepChanges(button) {
                var nextCount = Number( $nextStep.attr('data-step') ),
                    currentCount = Number( $currentStep.attr('data-step') ),
                    prevCount = Number( $prevStep.attr('data-step') );
                if ( button == 'next' ) {
                    $('.step-pane').removeClass('active');
                    $('.step-pane[data-step="'+(currentCount+1)+'"]').addClass('active');
                    // Update Counts
                    $nextStep.attr('data-step', nextCount+1 );
                    $currentStep.attr('data-step', currentCount+1 );
                    $prevStep.attr('data-step', prevCount+1 );
                    // Enable Previous Button
                    $prevStep.removeClass('disabled');
                    // Changing Next Step Name
                    $nextStepName.text( returnStepName(nextCount+1) );
                    // Changing Current Step Name & Number
                    $currentStepName.text( returnStepName(currentCount+1) );
                    // Changing Step Number
                    if ( nextCount != 7 ) {
                        $nextStepNumber.text( 'Step '+ (nextCount+1) );
                    }
                    $prevStepNumber.text( 'Step '+ (prevCount+1) );
                    $currentStepNumber.text( 'Step '+ (currentCount+1) );
                    if ( nextCount == 7 ) {
                        // Disable Next Button
                        // $nextStep.addClass('disabled');
                        $nextStepNumber.text( 'Finish' );
                    }
                }
                else if ( button == 'previous' ) {
                    $('.step-pane').removeClass('active');
                    $('.step-pane[data-step="'+(currentCount-1)+'"]').addClass('active');
                    // Update Counts
                    $nextStep.attr('data-step', nextCount-1 );
                    $currentStep.attr('data-step', currentCount-1 );
                    $prevStep.attr('data-step', prevCount-1 );
                    // Enable Next Button
                    $nextStep.removeClass('disabled');
                    // Changing Previous Step Name
                    $prevStepName.text( returnStepName(prevCount-1) );
                    // Changing Current Step Name & Number
                    $currentStepName.text( returnStepName(currentCount-1) );
                    // Changing Step Number
                    if ( prevCount != 1 ) {
                        $prevStepNumber.text( 'Step '+ (prevCount-1) );
                    }
                    $nextStepNumber.text( 'Step '+ (nextCount-1) );
                    $currentStepNumber.text( 'Step '+ (currentCount-1) );
                    if ( prevCount == 1 ) {
                        // Disable Previous Button
                        $prevStep.addClass('disabled');
                        $prevStepNumber.text( 'Start' );
                    }
                    else if ( prevCount == 4 ) {
                        deletedSBC = new Array();
                    }
                }
            }

            // Function To Return Current Step Name
            function returnStepName(count) {
                if ( count == 1 ) {
                    return 'Basic Information';
                }
                else if ( count == 2 ) {
                    return 'Attachment Config.';
                }
                else if ( count == 3 ) {
                    return 'Technical Config.';
                }
                else if ( count == 4 ) {
                    return 'Trunk Config.';
                }
                else if ( count == 5 ) {
                    return 'Auth. Rules Config.';
                }
                else if ( count == 6 ) {
                    return 'Rules';
                }
                else if ( count == 7 ) {
                    return 'Email Format';
                }
            }

            // Function For Old Wizard Functionality
            function oldWizard(count) {
                if (count == 1) {
                    var $form = $('#create_form');
                    formPost($form, count);
                    attachmentConfigDefaults();
                }
                else if (count == 2) {

                    var $form = $('#rate_sheet_conf_form');
                    formPost($form, count);

                    techConfigDefaultValues(true);
                    sbcChangeTrigger(true, 'technical_conf_form');
                    setTechCLDTranslation(true);

                    isSpecialCharValidation();
                    checkSelectedField('conf_sbc');
                    isNumericValidation('[name$="max_call"]');

                }
                else if (count == 3) {

                    var $form = $('#technical_conf_form');
                    $("#id_client_name").removeAttr('disabled');
                    formPost($form, count);
                    getSelectedSbcsForTrunk(true);
                    getRatePlan(true);
                    getTrunkProduct(true);
                    // checkSelectedField('trunk_type');
                    emptyPrefixChangeTrigger()
                    setAccordionCounterOnDelete($('#trunk_conf_form'));
                    trunkConfigIpMultipleSelect(true);

                    ClientTags = new clientIpsInit;
                    clientIpsInit();
                    SbcMultiselect(true);

                    /* Create Master Array for SBC */
                        $('[name="trunk-0-trunk_switch"] option').each(function(index, el) {
                            if ($(el).attr('value')) {
                                availableSbcs.push($(el).attr('value'));
                            }
                        });
                    /* Create Master Array for SBC -- End */

                }
                else if (count == 4) {
                    isNumericValidation('[name$="auth_incoming_cld"]');

                    var $form = $('#trunk_conf_form');
                    formPost($form, count);


                    getSelectedProducts(true);
                    authRulesIpMultipleSelect(true);
                    getAuthProduct(true);
                    getSelectedSbcs(true);
                    // sbcChangeTrigger(true, 'auth_rules_conf_form');
                    CreateDict()
                }
                else if (count == 5) {
                    var $form = $('#auth_rules_conf_form');
                    formPost($form, count);
                }
                else if (count == 6) {

                    var $form = $('#validation_rules_form');
                    formPost($form, count);

                    emailFormatDefaults();
                }
                else if (count == 7) {
                    finalStep();
                }
            }

            $('body').on('click', '.message .close', function(e) {
                $(this).closest('.message').transition('fade');

                $(this).find('input[type="radio"]').first().prop('checked', true);
            });

            function CreateDict () {
                var $form = $('form#trunk_conf_form')
                var CDict = []

                $form.find('.dynamic-formset2').each(function() {


                    var product_id = $(this).find('select[name$="trunk_type"]').val()
                    var sbc_id = $(this).find('select[name$="trunk_switch"]').val()
                    var trunk_prefix = $(this).find('[name$="trunk_prefix"]').val()
                    var trunk_ips = $(this).find('select[name$="trunk_ips"]').val()
                    if(trunk_prefix == "") {
                        var trunk_prefix = "None"
                    }

                    CDict.push([product_id, sbc_id, trunk_prefix, trunk_ips])
                    
                })

                fdata = {}
                $.each(CDict, function(idx, row){
                    if (!fdata.hasOwnProperty(row[0]))
                        fdata[row[0]] = {}
                    if ( row[1] ) {
                        $.each(row[1], function(idx, sbcId){
                            if (!fdata[row[0]].hasOwnProperty(sbcId)) {

                                fdata[row[0]][sbcId] = {}
                            }

                            if (!fdata[row[0]][sbcId].hasOwnProperty(row[2])) {
                                fdata[row[0]][sbcId][row[2]] = []
                            }

                            $.each(row[3], function(idx, ip){
                                if (fdata[row[0]][sbcId][row[2]].indexOf(ip) < 0) {
                                    fdata[row[0]][sbcId][row[2]].push(ip)
                                }
                            });
                        });
                    }
                });
                
            }

            function setDictForSBC (product, sbc, trunkPrefix, ips) {
                dicts[product][sbc][trunkPrefix] = new Array();
                $.each(ips, function(index, val) {
                    dicts[product][sbc][trunkPrefix].push(val);
                });

            }
            var dicts = {}

            function finalStep() {
                // allow order form to be submitted
                $('input:disabled, select:disabled').attr('data-disabled','disabled').removeAttr('disabled');
                var formData = $('#client_wizard form').serialize() + '&auth_trunk_prefix_list=' + encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(fdata));
                $.ajax({
                    "method": "POST",
                    "url": "/client_registration/complete/",
                    "data": formData,
                    "success": function(response) {
                        $('input[data-disabled="disabled"], select[data-disabled="disabled"]').attr('disabled','disabled');
                        $('p.help-block, .alert, .error.message').remove();
                        $('.error').removeClass('error');
                        $('#id_pocs_error_div').html('');
                        
                        var response = JSON.parse(response);
                        // var response = {"status": "SUCCESS", "1": {}, "2": {}, "3": {}, "4": {}, "5": {}, "6": {}, "7": {}}
                        // var response = {"status": "FAILED", "1": {}, "2": {}, "3": {"form-0-conf_sbc": ["Select a valid choice. 1 is not one of the available choices."]}, "4": {"trunk-0-trunk_switch": ["Select a valid choice. 1 is not one of the available choices."]}, "5": {"auth-0-auth_sbc": ["Select a valid choice. 1 is not one of the available choices."]}, "6": {}, "7": {}}
                        
                        if (response.status == 'SUCCESS') {
                            window.location.replace('/client_registration/completeredirection/'+companyID+'/');
                        }
                        else if (response.status == 'FAILED') {
                            delete response.status;
                            var pageID = [];
                            $.each(response,function(index, value) {
                                if (!$.isEmptyObject(value)) {
                                    pageID.push(Number(index));
                                    $.each(value, function(key, val) {
                                        if (key == 'pocs') {
                                            $('#id_pocs_error_div').text(val);
                                        }
                                        else if (key == 'non_field_error') {
                                            $('div.step-pane[data-step='+index+']').prepend('<div class="alert alert-error"><button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="alert">&times;</button><strong>Error! </strong>'+ val +'</div>');
                                        }
                                        else{
                                            $('.field:has([name='+key+'])').addClass('error');
                                            $('[name='+key+']').parent().append('<p class="help-block error">'+val+'</p>');
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            });
                            if ( pageID ) {
                                pageID = pageID.sort(function(a,b){return a - b});
                                var redirectStep = pageID[0]-1;
                                $nextStep.attr('data-step', redirectStep+1 );
                                $currentStep.attr('data-step', redirectStep );
                                $prevStep.attr('data-step', redirectStep-1 );
                                stepChanges('next');
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            /* Wizard Script - END */

            /* Add remove button for formset -- START */
                $('.delete-row').click(deleteRow);
            /* Add remove button for formset -- END */

                });

                    showDeptTrunk();
                    emptyPrefixChangeTrigger();
                    getSelectedSbcsForTrunk(false);
                    getRatePlan(false);
                    getTrunkProduct(false);

                    //~ $('[name$="trunk_type"]:last').change();

                    $.each(ips, function(index, val) {
                        $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"]:last').append('<option value="'+val+'">'+val+'</option>');
                    });

                    trunkConfigIpMultipleSelect(false);
                    SbcMultiselect(false);
                    //checkTrunkSBC();
                    bindSortselect();
                    $('.ui.checkbox').checkbox();

                });
                $('#auth_rules_conf_form a.add-row').click(function(event) {
                    isNumericValidation('[name$="auth_incoming_cld"]');
                    getSelectedProducts(false);
                    getSelectedSbcs(false);
                    getAuthProduct(false);
                    // sbcChangeTrigger(false, 'auth_rules_conf_form');
                    addAccordionCounter($('#auth_rules_conf_form'));
                    setAccordionCounterOnDelete($('#auth_rules_conf_form'));
                    $('#auth_rules_conf_form .accordion-group:not(:last)').removeClass('active');
                    var ips = ClientTags.client_ip_List.getTags();

                    isSpecialCharValidation();
                    // $.each(ips, function(index, val) {
                    //     $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_ips"]:last').append('<option value="'+val+'">'+val+'</option>');
                    // });
                    authRulesIpMultipleSelect(false);
                });
            /* Add Another Formset Actions - END */

        /* Generate POCs Table */
        function generatePocsTable(dep, val) {
            var resp = '<tr class="depart"><td colspan="6" style="padding: 0;" data-responsive="hide"><strong>'+dep+'</strong></td></tr>';
            $.each(val, function(index, value) {
                resp = resp + '<tr><td align="center" data-responsive="hide"><div class="ui checkbox small">';
                    resp += '<input type="checkbox" name="pocs" value="'+value.id+'" class="hidden">';
                    resp += '<label></label></div></td>'+
                    '<td data-title="First Name">'+value.first_name+'</td>'+
                    '<td data-title="Last Name">'+value.last_name+'</td>'+
                    '<td data-title="Email">'+value.contact_email+'</td>'+
                    '<td data-title="Fax">'+value.fax_number+'</td>'+
                '</tr>';
            });
            return resp;
        }
        /* Generate POCs Table - END */

        /* Attachment Config. Defaults */
            function attachmentConfigDefaults () {
                var $attachment_form = $('#rate_sheet_conf_form');
                $attachment_form.find('[name="invoice_template"], [name="ratesheet_full"], [name="ratesheet_partial"], [name="ratesheet_atoz"], [name="ratesheet_dial_code"]').val($(this).find("option:first").attr('value'));

                $('#id_invoice_template_preview').click();
            }

        /* Client Tech Conf. IP Wigdet Script */
            function clientIpsInit(){

                var ips = '';
                Tags.bootstrapVersion = "2";

                this.client_ip_List = $('#client_ips').tags({
                    tagSize: "sm",
                    tagClass: "btn-primary",
                    promptText: " Press enter to add IP addresses",
                    numaricField: true,
                    afterAddingTag: function (tag) {

                        if (!validateIp(tag) || tag == "255.255.255.255" || tag == "0.0.0.0") {
                            client_ip_List.removeTag(tag);
                            if ($('#validClientIPError').length == 0) {
                                $('#clientIPsTitle').append('<span id="validClientIPError" class="label label-important" style="padding: 0px;">Enter Valid IP!</span>');
                            };
                        }
                        else{
                            $('#validClientIPError').remove();

                            ips = client_ip_List.getTags();

                            $('[name="client_ips"]').val(ips);

                            $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"]')
                                .append('<option value="'+tag+'">'+tag+'</option>');

                            $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"]').multipleSelect('refresh');

                            $('#clear_ips').click(function(event) {
                                if (ips.length != 0) {
                                    $.each(ips, function(index, ip) {
                                        client_ip_List.removeTag(ip);
                                        client_ip_List.removeLastTag();
                                    });
                                };
                            });
                        }
                    },
                    afterDeletingTag: function (tag) {
                        $('[name="client_ips"]').val(ips);
                        $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"] option')
                        .each(function(index, el) {
                            if ($(this).attr('value') == tag) {
                                $(this).remove();
                            }
                        });
                        $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"]').multipleSelect('refresh');
                    }
                });
                $('#client_ips textarea').css('width','100%');
            }
        /* Client Tech Conf. IP Wigdet Script- END */

        /* Generate IPs Range */
            function generateIpsRange(ClientsTagsIns) {

                var clientIpsRange = $('#id_client_ip_range').val().trim();
                var getPreTags = [];

                if (anyChar(clientIpsRange) || (clientIpsRange == '' && $('#ips_range').is(':checked'))) {
                    $('.label-important').remove();
                    if ($('#invalidAnyChar').length == 0) { // check error element is exist or not
                        $('#id_client_ip_range').parent().append('<p id="invalidAnyChar" class="label label-important" style="padding: 0px;">Please! Enter a valid Format.</p>');
                    }
                }
                else{
                    $('.label-important').remove();

                    try {
                        var ipsList = clientIpsRange.split(',');

                        $.each(ipsList, function(i, val) {

                            var ipRange = ipsList[i].split('-');

                            var ipArr = ipRange[0].split('.');

                            var ipFromEnd = ipArr.pop();
                            var ipToEnd = ipRange[1];

                            var ipInitials = ipArr.toString().replace(/,/g , ".");

                            if ($('#ips_range').is(':checked')) {

                                var ipFrom = ipRange[0].trim();
                                var ipTo = ipInitials.trim()+'.'+ipRange[1].trim();
                            }
                            else if ($('#ips_cidr').is(':checked')) {

                                var result = IpSubnetCalculator.calculateSubnetMask(
                                    $( '#subnet_ip' ).val(),
                                    $( '#subnet_prefix' ).val()
                                );

                                if( result === null ){
                                }
                                else{
                                    var ipFrom = result.ipLowStr;
                                    var ipTo = result.ipHighStr;

                                    var ipasplit = ipFrom.split(".")
                                    ipasplit[3] ++;

                                    ipFrom = ipasplit.join(".")


                                    var ipasplit = ipTo.split(".")
                                    ipasplit[3] --;
                                    
                                    ipTo = ipasplit.join(".")

                                }
                            }

                            if ((!validateIp(ipFrom) || !validateIp(ipTo)) && $('#ips_range').is(':checked')){ //IP Validation
                                if ($('#invalidIpError').length == 0) { // check error element is exist or not
                                    $('#id_client_ip_range').parent().append('<p id="invalidIpError" class="label label-important" style="padding: 0px;">Sorry! Enter a valid IP address!</p>');
                                };
                            }
                            else {
                                $('.label-important').remove();

                                if (Number(ipFromEnd) > Number(ipToEnd)) { // Check if IP Range is valid or not

                                    if ($('#invalidIpRangeError').length == 0) { // check error element is exist or not
                                        $('#id_client_ip_range').parent().append('<p id="invalidIpRangeError" class="label label-important" style="padding: 0px;">Please! Give the suitable range.</p>');
                                    }
                                }
                                else {
                                    $('.label-important').remove();

                                    function ipToHex(ip) {
                                        var d = ip.split('.');
                                        return ((((((+d[0])*256)+(+d[1]))*256)+(+d[2]))*256)+(+d[3]);
                                    }

                                    for(var i = ipToHex(ipFrom); i <= ipToHex(ipTo); i++){

                                        var oc4 = (i>>24) & 0xff;
                                        var oc3 = (i>>16) & 0xff;
                                        var oc2 = (i>>8) & 0xff;
                                        var oc1 = i & 0xff;

                                        var ips = oc4 + "." + oc3 + "." + oc2 + "." + oc1;

                                        ClientsTagsIns.client_ip_List.addTag(ips);

                                    } //forloop
                                    $('#addIpModal').bodal('hide'); //dissmiss modal

                                } // range validation
                            } //ip validation
                        }); //parent eachloop
                    }
                    catch(err) {
                        if ($('#catch_error').length == 0) { // check error element is exist or not
                            $('#addIpModal').find('.content').append('<span id="catch_error" class="label label-important pull-left" style="padding: 0px;">Sorry! something went wrong. Please enter a valid format.</span>');
                        }

                    }
                }
                $('#getIpsRange').removeClass('disabled loading');
            }
        /* Generate IPs Range - END */

        function checkSelectedField(field) {
            var thisField = '[name*="'+field+'"]';
            $(thisField).change(function(){

                // start by setting everything to enabled
                $(thisField).find('option').show();
                // loop each select and set the selected value to disabled in all other selects
                $(thisField).each(function(){
                    var $this = $(this);
                    $(thisField).not($this).find('option').each(function(){
                       if($(this).attr('value') == $this.val())
                           $(this).hide();
                    });
                });
            });
            $('a.delete-row').click(function(){
                thisField = '[name*="'+field+'"]';
                $(thisField).find('option').show();
                // loop each select and set the selected value to disabled in all other selects
                $(thisField).each(function(){
                    var $this = $(this);
                    $(thisField).not($this).find('option').each(function(){
                       if($(this).attr('value') == $this.val())
                           $(this).hide();
                    });
                });
            });
        }

        /* Technical Config. Fields' Default Values */
            function techConfigDefaultValues(flag) {
                var which = flag?':first':':last';
                $('.client_ip_conf'+which+' [name$="credit_limit"]').val(2);
                $('.client_ip_conf'+which+' [name$="max_session_time"]').val(7200);
                $('.client_ip_conf'+which+' [name$="max_session"]').val(2);
                $('.client_ip_conf'+which+' [name$="max_call"]').val('unlimited');
                $('.client_ip_conf'+which+' select[name$="prefered_codec"]').val($(this).closest("option:first").val());
            }
        /* Technical Config. Fields' Default Values - END */

        function getSelectedSbcs(flag) {
            var options = '<option selected="" value="">-------</option>';
            $('#trunk_conf_form').find('select[name$="trunk_switch"]').each(function(index, el) {
                $(el).find('option:selected').each(function(i, e){
                    options += $(e).prop('outerHTML');
                });
            });
            if (flag) {
                $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_sbc"]').each(function(index, el) {
                    $(el).html(options);
                });

            }else{
                $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_sbc"]:last').html(options);
            }
            $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_sbc"]').each(function(index, el) {
                $(el).find('option').each(function(){
                    $(this).siblings("[value="+ this.value+"]").remove();
                });
            });
        }
        function getSelectedSbcsForTrunk(flag) {
            var selectedSBCs = [];
            $('#technical_conf_form').find('[name$="conf_sbc"]').each(function(index, elem) {
                selectedSBCs.push($(elem).find('option:checked').attr('value'));
            });

            if(deletedSBC.length > 0) {
                $.each(deletedSBC, function(index, val) {
                    $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_switch"]').each(function(){
                        $(this).find('option[value="'+val+'"]').prop({'selected': false, 'disabled' : 'disabled'});

                    })
                });
            }
            $.each(selectedSBCs, function(index, foo) { // [1, 2]
                $('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_switch"] option[value="'+foo+'"]').attr('disabled', false);
            });
        }
        function getRoutingGroupOptions(flag) {
            var routingGroupOptions = flag?$('#technical_conf_form [name$="routing_group"]').prop('innerHTML'):$('#technical_conf_form [name$="routing_group"]:last').prop('innerHTML');
            $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="routing_group"]:last').html(routingGroupOptions);
        }
        var ratePlanObj = '';
        function getRatePlan(flag) {
            if (flag) {
                $.get('/client_registration/getrateplan/', function(res){
                    var res = JSON.parse(res);
                    ratePlanObj = res;
                    trunkTypeChange($('#trunk_conf_form [name$="trunk_type"]'), ratePlanObj);
                });
            }
            else{
                trunkTypeChange($('#trunk_conf_form [name$="trunk_type"]'), ratePlanObj);
            }
        }

        function setIpsBySbc (trunk, value, ips) {
            dict[trunk][value] = new Array();
            $.each(ips, function(index, val) {
                dict[trunk][value].push(val);
            });
        }
        var dict = {};

        function trunkTypeChange (elem, res) {
            $(elem).change(function(event) {

                var that = $(this);
                var options = '';
                if(res.hasOwnProperty($(this).val())) {
                    $.each(res[$(this).val()], function(index, value) {
                        options += '<option value="'+value[0]+'">'+value[1]+'</option>';
                        $(that).parents('.accordion-group:first').find('[name$="rate_plan"]').html(options);
                    });
                }else {
                   $(that).parents('.accordion-group:first').find('[name$="rate_plan"]').html("");
                }

            });
        }

        function deleteRow(){
            $('[name$="trunk_switch"],[name$="trunk_ips"],[name$="auth_ips"]').multipleSelect('refresh');
        }
        function getSelectedProducts(flag) {

            var selectedProducts = '<option selected value="" data-prefix="" data-trunkprefix="">-------</option>';
            $('#trunk_conf_form [name$="trunk_type"]').each(function(index, el) {
                var trunk_prefix = $(el).parent().closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="trunk_prefix"]').val();
                var empty_billing_prefix = $(el).parent().closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="trunk_empty_prefix"]').val();
                if($(el).val() != '') {
                    selectedProducts += $(el).find('option:checked').attr({'data-trunkprefix': trunk_prefix, 'data-empty_prefix': empty_billing_prefix}).prop('outerHTML');
                }
            });
            if (flag) {
                $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_product"]').html(selectedProducts);
            }
            else{
                $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_product"]:last').html(selectedProducts);
            }

            $('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_product"]').each(function(index, el) {
                if (!$(el).val()) {
                    $(el).closest('.dynamic-formset3').find('[name$="auth_sbc"]').prop('disabled', true).val('');
                    $(el).closest('.dynamic-formset3').find('select[name$="auth_ips"]').html('');
                };
                $(el).find('option').each(function(){
                    $(this).siblings("[value="+ this.value+"]").remove();
                });
            });
        }
        function getTrunkProduct(flag) {
            var elem = flag?$('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_type"]:first'):$('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_type"]:last');
            $(elem).change(function(event) {
                var text = $(this).find('option:selected').text();
                var prefix = $(this).find(':selected').attr('data-prefix');

                var $TrunkSwitch = $(this).parents('.dynamic-formset2:first').find('select[name$="trunk_switch"]');
                var $TrunkIp = $(this).parents('.dynamic-formset2:first').find('select[name$="trunk_ips"]');
                var selectedTrunk = $(this).parents('.dynamic-formset2:first').find('select[name$="trunk_type"]').val();

                $(this).closest('.accordion-group').find('.accordion-toggle').text(text.toUpperCase());
                $(this).closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="billing_prefix"]').val(prefix);

                $TrunkSwitch.val('').multipleSelect('refresh');
                if ($(this).val()) {
                    $TrunkSwitch.multipleSelect('enable');
                }
                else{
                    // Set Sbc Multiselect in a default state
                    $.each(dict, function(product, sbc) {
                        delete dict[product][$TrunkSwitch.val()];
                    });
                    $TrunkSwitch.multipleSelect('disable');
                    $TrunkSwitch.parent().find('.ms-drop label').show();
                    $TrunkSwitch.multipleSelect('uncheckAll');

                    $TrunkIp.multipleSelect('uncheckAll');
                }
            });
        }
        function getAuthProduct(flag) {
            var elem = flag?$('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_product"]:first'):$('#auth_rules_conf_form [name$="auth_product"]:last');

            $(elem).unbind().change(function(event) {

                var trunk_prefix = '', billing_prefix = '', incoming_cld = '', empty_billing_prefix = '';

                var authProduct = $(this).val();
                var name = $(this).attr('name');
                var $thisParent = $(elem).parents('div.accordion-inner')
                var $AuthSbc = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_sbc"]');
                var $authTrunkPrefix = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_trunk_prefix"]');
                var $authIPs = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_ips"]');

                $thisParent.find('[name$="routing_group"]').html('')

                $AuthSbc.val('')
                $AuthSbc.prop('disabled', true);

                $authTrunkPrefix.val('')
                $authTrunkPrefix.prop('disabled', true);

                $authIPs.val('')
                $authIPs.multipleSelect('refresh').multipleSelect('disable');

                if(authProduct) {
                    // Disabled and Hide all the options in Auth SBC Dropdown
                    $AuthSbc.find('option').attr('disabled','disabled').hide();

                    $.each(fdata[authProduct],function(key, value){
                        $AuthSbc.find('option[value="'+key+'"]').removeAttr('disabled').show()
                    });
                    // Enable Auth SBC Dropdown if product value is true
                    $AuthSbc.prop('disabled', false);
                    $AuthSbc.unbind().change(function(){
                        var options = '<option value="">-- Select Trunk Prefix --</option>'
                        var selectedSBC = $(this).val();
                        var name = $(this).attr('name');
                        var trunkList = fdata[authProduct][selectedSBC];

                        if(selectedSBC) {
                            $.each(trunkList, function(key, value){
                                options += '<option value="'+key+'">'+key+'</option>';
                            });

                            $authTrunkPrefix.html(options);
                            $authIPs.multipleSelect('refresh').multipleSelect('disable');

                            $authTrunkPrefix.prop('disabled', false);

                            cldTranslationCreation($(this))

                            getRoutingGroup(name, selectedSBC, true);
                        }
                        else {
                            $authTrunkPrefix.html('');
                        }
                    });

                    $authTrunkPrefix.unbind().change(function(){
                        var options = ''
                        var selectedSBC = $(this).parents('div.accordion-inner').find('[name$="auth_sbc"]').val()
                        var trunkVal = $(this).val()
                        var IpsList = fdata[authProduct][selectedSBC][trunkVal]

                        $.each(IpsList, function(index, value){
                            options += '<option value="'+value+'">'+value+'</option>'
                        });

                        if(trunkVal){
                            $authIPs.html(options);
                            $authIPs.multipleSelect('refresh').multipleSelect('enable');
                            // $modalForm.find('#routingGroup').removeAttr('disabled');
                            cldTranslationCreation($(this))
                        }
                        else {
                            $authIPs.html('');
                            $authIPs.multipleSelect('refresh').multipleSelect('disable')

                            // $modalForm.find('#routingGroup').html('').attr('disabled')
                            // $modalForm.find('#routingGroup').attr('disabled','disabled')
                        }
                    });

                    cldTranslationCreation($(this))
                }





                billing_prefix = $(this).closest('.dynamic-formset3').find('[name$="auth_product"] option:selected').attr('data-prefix');
                incoming_cld = $(this).closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="auth_incoming_cld"]').val();

                if ($(this).attr('name').indexOf('auth_product') >= 0) {
                    var text = $(this).find('option:selected').text();
                    $(this).closest('.accordion-group').find('.accordion-toggle').text(text.toUpperCase());
                }

                $('[name$="auth_incoming_cld"]').unbind().on('keyup',function() {
                    cldTranslationCreation($(this))
                })

                function cldTranslationCreation(argument) {
                    var $thisParent = $(argument).parents('div.accordion-inner')
                    var inc_cld = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_incoming_cld"]').val();
                    var auth_product = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_product"]').val();
                    var empty_billing_prefix = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_product"]').find('option:selected').attr('data-empty_prefix');

                    if (auth_product) {
                        var trunk_prefix = $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_trunk_prefix"]').val();
                        
                        if(trunk_prefix){
                            if( trunk_prefix.indexOf("+") > -1 ){ 
                                // Found "+" Sign in trunk Prefix
                                var newTrunkPrefix = trunk_prefix.replace("+", "[+]")
                                trunk_prefix = newTrunkPrefix
                            }
                        }

                        if(trunk_prefix == "None" || trunk_prefix == "") {
                            var trunk_prefix = ""
                        }
                        // var billing_prefix = productObj[auth_product][1];

                        if(empty_billing_prefix == "false"){
                            $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_cld_translation"]').val('s/^'+trunk_prefix+billing_prefix+inc_cld+'/'+billing_prefix+inc_cld+'/');
                        }else {
                            $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_cld_translation"]').val('s/^'+trunk_prefix+inc_cld+'/'+billing_prefix+inc_cld+'/');
                        }

                    }
                    else{
                        $thisParent.find('[name$="auth_cld_translation"]').val('');
                    }
                }

            });
            
        }

        function authRulesIpMultipleSelect(flag) {
            var $AuthIps = flag?$('#auth_rules_conf_form select[name$="auth_ips"]'):$('#auth_rules_conf_form select[name$="auth_ips"]:last');
            $AuthIps.multipleSelect({
                placeholder: "Select IPs",
                filter: true
            }).multipleSelect('disable');
        }
        function trunkConfigIpMultipleSelect(flag) {
            var $TrunkIps = flag?$('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"]:first'):$('#trunk_conf_form select[name$="trunk_ips"]:last');
            var selectedTrunk = '', selectedSbcs = '';

            $TrunkIps.multipleSelect({
                placeholder: "Select IPs",
                filter: true,
                onOpen: function () {
                    selectedTrunk = $TrunkIps.parent().parent().find('select[name$="trunk_type"]').val();
                },
                onClick: function (view) {
                    selectedSbcs = $TrunkIps.parent().parent().find('select[name$="trunk_switch"]').multipleSelect('getSelects');
                    if (selectedTrunk && dict.hasOwnProperty(selectedTrunk)) {
                        if (view.checked) {
                            $.each(selectedSbcs, function(i, sbc) {
                                if ($.inArray(view.value, dict[selectedTrunk][sbc]) == -1) {
                                    dict[selectedTrunk][sbc].push(view.value);
                                };
                            });
                        }else{
                            $.each(selectedSbcs, function(i, sbc) {
                                dict[selectedTrunk][sbc].splice(dict[selectedTrunk][sbc].indexOf(view.value), 1);
                            })
                        }
                    };
                },
                onCheckAll: function() {
                    if (selectedTrunk) {
                        var allIps = $TrunkIps.multipleSelect('getSelects');
                        selectedSbcs = $TrunkIps.parent().parent().find('select[name$="trunk_switch"]').multipleSelect('getSelects');
                    }
                },
                onUncheckAll: function() {
                    if (selectedTrunk) {
                        selectedSbcs = $TrunkIps.parent().parent().find('select[name$="trunk_switch"]').multipleSelect('getSelects');
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        /* Populate Trunk Ips multipleSelect - END */

        function sbcChangeTrigger(flag, form_id){
            var elem = '';
            if (form_id === 'technical_conf_form') {
                elem = flag?$('#technical_conf_form select[name$="conf_sbc"]:first'):$('#technical_conf_form select[name$="conf_sbc"]:last');
            }
            else if(form_id === 'auth_rules_conf_form'){
                elem = flag?$('#auth_rules_conf_form select[name$="auth_sbc"]:first'):$('#auth_rules_conf_form select[name$="auth_sbc"]:last');
            }

            $(elem).change(function(){
                var name = $(this).attr('name');
                var value = $(this).val();
                var text = $(this).find('option:selected').text();

                if(name.indexOf('conf_sbc') >= 0) {
                    $(this).closest('.accordion-group').find('.accordion-heading>a').text(text.toUpperCase());
                }
                else if (name.indexOf('auth_sbc') >= 0){
                    var auth_product = $(this).parent().parent().find('select[name$="auth_product"]').val();
                    var auth_sbc = $(this).val();
                    var options = '';
                    var ips = dict[auth_product][auth_sbc];
                    if (auth_product && auth_sbc) {
                        $.each(ips, function(i, ip) {
                            options += '<option value="'+ip+'">'+ip+'</option>';
                        });
                    }
                    $(this).parent().parent().find('select[name$="auth_ips"]').html(options).multipleSelect('refresh').multipleSelect('enable');
                }
                $('.collapse:has([name='+name+']) [name$="client_class"]').html('<option selected value="">-------</option>');
                $('.collapse:has([name='+name+']) select[name$="prefered_codec"]').html('<option selected value="">-------</option>');

                if(value){

                    var data = AccountClassesData[value];
                    var selectOptions = '';
                    for(var i in data){
                        selectOptions += '<option value="'+data[i][0]+'">'+data[i][1]+'</option>';
                    };
                    $('.collapse:has([name='+name+']) [name$="client_class"]').html(selectOptions);


                    var data = PrefferedCodecData[value];
                    var selectOptions = '';
                    for(var i in data){
                        selectOptions += '<option value="'+data[i][0]+'">'+data[i][1]+'</option>';
                    }
                    $('.collapse:has([name='+name+']) select[name$="prefered_codec"]').html(selectOptions);

                    var data = MediaRelayData[value];
                    var selectOptions = '';
                    for(var i in data){
                        selectOptions += '<option value="'+data[i][0]+'">'+data[i][1]+'</option>';
                    }
                    $('.collapse:has([name='+name+']) [name$="media_relay_type"]').html(selectOptions);
                    getRoutingGroup(name, value, true);
                }
            });
        }
        function setTechCLDTranslation(flag){
            var elem = flag?$('[name$="auth_billing_prefix"]'):$('[name$="auth_billing_prefix"]:last');
            $(elem).on('change keyup', function(){

                var empty_prefix = $(elem).find('[name$="auth_empty_prefix"]').is(':checked');

                var billing_prefix = $(this).val();
                billing_prefix = isNumeric(billing_prefix)?billing_prefix:'';

                var product = !empty_prefix?billing_prefix:'';

                $(this).closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="cld_translation"]').val('s/^'+product+'/'+billing_prefix+'/');
            });
        }
        function isNumericValidation(elem) {
            $(elem).on('keyup', function(event) {
                var val = $(this).val(), $Parent = $(this).parent(), $that = $(this);
                $Parent.removeClass('error');
                $Parent.find('.isnum-error').remove();

                if (!$(this).is(':disabled')) {
                    if (val != '' && !isNumeric(val)) {

                        if ($(this).attr('name').toLowerCase().indexOf("max_call") >= 0) {
                            if (val != 'unlimited') {
                                $Parent.addClass('error').append('<p class="help-block isnum-error">Numbers or "unlimited" allowed.</p>');
                            };
                        }
                        else {

                            $that.val($that.val().replace(/[^0-9]/g, function(str){ 
                                $('.help-block').remove();
                                $Parent.addClass('error');
                                $that.after('<p class="help-block isnum-error">Only numbers allowed.</p>')
                            return ''; }));
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                $Parent.removeClass('error'); 
                                $('.help-block').remove();
                            },1500)
                        }
                    }
                    else if (isNumeric(val)){
                        setTimeout(function(){
                            $Parent.removeClass('error');
                            $('.help-block').remove();
                        },1500)
                        
                    }
                };
            });
        }
        function isSpecialCharValidation() {
            $('[name$="cld_translationd"], [name$="auth_cli_translation"], [name$="auth_cli_translation"]')
                .on('keyup change', function(event) {
                var val = $(this).val(), $Parent = $(this).parent();
                $Parent.removeClass('error');
                $Parent.find('.isspchar-error').remove();

                if (!isSpecialChar(val) && val != '') {

                    $Parent.addClass('error').append('<p class="help-block isspchar-error">You may type rule like "s/^123/123/"</p>');
                }
                else if (isSpecialChar(val)){
                    $Parent.removeClass('error');
                }
            });
        }
        function emptyPrefixChangeTrigger(){
            $('[name$="trunk_empty_prefix"]').change(function(event) {
                if ($(this).is(':checked')) {
                    $(this).val(true);
                }
                else {
                    $(this).val(false);
                }

                var empty_prefix = $(this).is(':checked');
            });
        }
        function getRoutingGroup (name, value, isSbcChange) {
            if(value) {
                if(RoutingGroupData.hasOwnProperty(value)){
                    var data = RoutingGroupData[value];
                    data = data.sort((function(index){
                        return function(a, b){
                            return (a[index] === b[index] ? 0 : (a[index] < b[index] ? -1 : 1));
                        };
                    })(1));
                    var selectOptions = '';
                    for(var i in data){
                        selectOptions += '<option value="'+data[i][0]+'">'+data[i][1]+'</option>';
                    }
                    $('[name='+name+']').closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="routing_group"]').html(selectOptions);
                    if (isSbcChange) {
                        $('.collapse:has([name='+name+'])').find('[id$="trunk_delete_row"]').parent()
                            .find('[name$="routing_group"]').html(selectOptions);

                    }else{
                        $('.collapse:has([name='+name+'])').find('[id$="trunk_delete_row"]').parent()
                            .find('[name$="routing_group"]:last').html(selectOptions);
                    }
                }
            }
            else {
                $('[name='+name+']').closest('.accordion-group').find('[name$="routing_group"]').html('');
            }
        }


        function addAccordionCounter(form) {
            var id = $(form).find('.accordion-body:last').attr('id');
            $(form).find('.accordion-group:last').find('a.accordion-toggle').attr('href','#'+id);
            emptyPrefixChangeTrigger();

                $('.delete-row').click(deleteRow);

        }
        function isNumeric(input) {
            var re = /^\d+$/;
            return re.test(input);
        }
        function isSpecialChar(input) {
            var re = /[^A-Za-z0-9\-_]/;
            return re.test(input);
        }
        function anyChar(input) {
            var re = /[a-zA-Z]+/;
            return re.test(input);
        }
        function validateEmail(email) {
            var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
            return re.test(email);
        }
        function validateIp(ip) {
            var re = /^(([0-9]|[1-9][0-9]|1[0-9]{2}|2[0-4][0-9]|25[0-5])\.){3}([0-9]|[1-9][0-9]|1[0-9]{2}|2[0-4][0-9]|25[0-5])$/;
            return re.test(ip);
        }
        function formPost(form, step) {
            form.find('input:disabled, select:disabled').attr('data-disabled','disabled').removeAttr('disabled');

            var data = form.serialize() + '&auth_trunk_prefix_list=' + encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(fdata));

                // var data = $('#auth_rules_conf_form').serialize() + '&auth_trunk_prefix_list=' + JSON.stringify(fdata);
            $.ajax( {
                type: "POST",
                url: form.attr( 'action' ),
                data: data,
                success: function( response ) {
                    form.find('input[data-disabled="disabled"], select[data-disabled="disabled"]').attr('disabled','disabled');
                    form.find('p.help-block, .alert').remove();
                    $('.error.message').remove();
                    form.find('.error').removeClass('error');
                    var data = $.parseJSON(response);
                    if (!$.isEmptyObject(data)) {
                        $('#id_pocs_error_div').html('');
                        $.each(data, function(key, val) {
                            if (key == 'pocs') {
                                form.find('#id_pocs_error_div').text(val);
                            }
                            else if (key == 'non_field_error') {
                                $(form).parent('div.step-pane').prepend('<div class="ui error message"><i class="close icon"></i><div class="header">There were some errors with your submission</div><ul class="list"><li>'+ val +'</li></ul></div>');
                            }
                            else{
                                $('.control-group:has([name='+key+'])').addClass('error');
                                $('[name='+key+']').parent().append('<p class="help-block error">'+val+'</p>');
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    else if($.isEmptyObject(data)) {
                        stepChanges('next');
                        // $('#client_wizard').wizard('selectedItem',{step: step+1});
                        form.find('p.help-block').remove();
                        form.find('#id_pocs_error_div').html('');
                    }
                },
                error: function (response) {
                    form.find('input[data-disabled="disabled"]').attr('disabled','disabled');
                }
            });
        }
        function setAccordionCounterOnDelete(form) {
            $('a.delete-row').click(function(event) {
                $(form).find('.accordion-body').each(function(index, el) {
                    $(el).closest('.accordion-group').find('a.accordion-toggle').attr('href', '#'+$(el).attr('id'));
                });
                // Delete Selected SBCs in trunk_conf_form
                if ($(form).attr('id') == 'trunk_conf_form') {
                    var trunk_type = $(this).parent('.dynamic-formset2').find('[name$="trunk_type"]').val();
                    var trunk_switch = $(this).parent('.dynamic-formset2').find('[name$="trunk_switch"]').val();
                    if (trunk_switch != null) {
                        $.each(trunk_switch, function(i, sbc) {
                            delete dict[trunk_type][sbc];
                        });
                    };
                }
                else if ($(form).attr('id') == 'technical_conf_form') {
                    var conf_sbc = $(this).parent('.dynamic-formset1').find('[name$="conf_sbc"]').val();

                    if($.inArray(conf_sbc, deletedSBC) == -1) {
                        deletedSBC.push(conf_sbc)
                    }
                    $.each(dict, function(product, obj) {
                        delete dict[product][conf_sbc];
                    });
                }
            });
        }
        function tabsRunning() {
            $('.ui.tabular.menu div').click(function () {
                var tabNAme = $(this).attr('data-tab');
                $(this).parent().find('div').removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass('active');

                $(this).parents('#id_tempPreview').find('.ui.tab').removeClass('active');
                $(this).parents('#id_tempPreview').find('.ui.tab[data-tab="'+tabNAme+'"]').addClass('active');
            });
            $('.ui.tabular.menu div:first').click();
        }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        function responsiveTable(elem) {
            $(elem).find(".ba-table:not(.no-responsive) tbody tr").each(function () {
                var $firstTd = $(this).find("td:first-child:not(.dataTables_empty)")
                var $secondTd = $(this).find("td:eq(1)");

                var trButtonLenght = $(this).find('span.tr-button').length;

                if(!trButtonLenght) {
                    if($firstTd.attr('data-responsive') == "hide"){
                        $secondTd.append("<span class='tr-button'></span>")
                    }
                    else {
                        $firstTd.append("<span class='tr-button'></span>");
                    }
                }

            });

            $(elem).find(".ba-table:not(.no-responsivetr-button) tbody tr .tr-button").off().on("click",function(){
                $(this).toggleClass("open").parent().parent().toggleClass("open");
            });
        }

        // Ajax Loader

        xhrPool = [];
        $.ajaxSetup({
            beforeSend: function(jqXHR) {
                xhrPool.push(jqXHR);
            }
        })
        $(document).ajaxStart(function () {
            $('#pre_loader').remove();
            $('body').prepend('<div class="ui active dimmer" id="pre_loader"><div><img src="/static/img/BitsAutoLogoAnimation-6.gif" width="80" />Loading ...</div></div>');
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('#cancelAjax').show()
                $('#cancelAjax').click(function() {
                    $.each(xhrPool, function(idx, jqXHR) {
                        jqXHR.abort();
                    });
                    xhrPool = [];
                })
            }, 1000);
         })
         .ajaxStop(function () {
            $('#pre_loader').remove();
        })
        .ajaxError(function(e, error) {
            var modalLen = $('body').find('.modal.active').length
            var $modalBox = $('body').find('.modal.active')
            var modalActionLen = $modalBox.find('div.actions').length
            var modalContentLen = $modalBox.find('div.content').length
            var dividerLen = $('.ui.divider.dotted').length
            // First remove Backend Error
            $('#backendError').remove();
            if(modalLen > 0) {
                if(modalActionLen > 0) {
                    $modalBox.find('div.actions').prepend('<span class="ui message negative"  id="backendError"><strong>ERROR!!!</strong> '+error.status+': '+error.statusText+'</span>');
                }
                else if(modalContentLen > 0){
                    $modalBox.find('div.content').prepend('<span class="ui message negative"  id="backendError"><strong>ERROR!!!</strong> '+error.status+': '+error.statusText+'</span>');
                }
            }
            else if(dividerLen > 0){
                // Show Backend Error
                $('.ui.divider.dotted').after('<div class="ui negative message" id="backendError"><strong>ERROR!!!</strong> '+error.status+': '+error.statusText+'</div>');
            }
            else {
                // Show Backend Error
                $('div.pusher').find('.ui.container:first').prepend('<div class="ui negative message" id="backendError"><strong>ERROR!!!</strong> '+error.status+': '+error.statusText+'</div>');

            }
            $(".ui.button.loading").removeClass( 'disabled loading' );
            // Remove Backend Error After 5 seconds
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('#backendError').remove();
            },5000);
        });



        $(document).ready(function () {
            if(xhrPool.length == 0){
                $('#pre_loader').remove();
            }
        });

        function status_modal_client(i, clientName){
            var elem = $('#id_client_switch_modal').bodal({
                blurring: true,
                onShow: function () {
                    $.ajax({
                        method:'get',
                        url:'/corporate/switch_account_mapping/'+ i + '/',
                        success:function(data) {
                            $('#id_client_switch_modal').html(data);
                            $('#id_client_switch_modal .loader').addClass('hide');
                            $('#id_client_switch_modal .ui.dimmer').addClass('hide');

                                responsiveTable(elem);

                            // Semantic UI [popup == ToolTip]
                            $('.ui.modle .inline.icon, .ui.modle .ba-table tbody tr td > span').popup({
                                inline: true
                            });
                        }
                    });
                }
            })
            .bodal('setting', 'closable', false)
            .bodal('show');
        };

        function status_modal_invoice_form(i){
             $.ajax({
                method:'get',
                url:'/invoices/vendorinvoice/'+ i +'/enter_vendorinvoice/',
                success:function(data) {
                    $('#id_vendor_invoice_form_modal .description').html(data);

                    var elem = $('#id_vendor_invoice_form_modal').bodal({
                        blurring: true,
                        onShow: function () {
                            $('#id_vendor_invoice_form_modal .loader').addClass('hide');
                            $('#id_vendor_invoice_form_modal .ui.dimmer').addClass('hide');
                            responsiveTable(elem);
                        }
                    })
                    .bodal('setting', 'closable', false)
                    .bodal('show')
                }
            });
        };

        function status_modal_payment(i){
            var elem = $('#id_payment_switch_modal').bodal({
                blurring: true,
                onShow: function () {
                    $.ajax({
                        method:'get',
                        url:'/payments/payment/sbc_wise_payment/'+ i + '/',
                        success:function(data) {
                            $('#id_payment_switch_modal').html(data);
                            $('#id_payment_switch_modal .loader').addClass('hide');
                            $('#id_payment_switch_modal .ui.dimmer').addClass('hide');

                                responsiveTable(elem);

                            // Semantic UI [popup == ToolTip]
                            $('.ui.modle .inline.icon, .ui.modle .ba-table tbody tr td > span').popup({
                                inline: true
                            });
                        }
                    });
                }
            })
            .bodal('setting', 'closable', false)
            .bodal('show');
        };
        // Function for Compnay SBC Status Modal Semantic-Ui
        function status_modal(i){
             var elem = $('#id_company_status_modal').bodal({
                blurring: true,
                onShow: function () {
                    $.ajax({
                        method:'get',
                        dataType:'json',
                        url:'/switch_api/'+i+'/',
                        success:function(data){
                            var reseller = false;
                            var client = false;
                            var st_red = '<i class="icon-circle" style="background:red"></i>';
                            var st_green = '<i class="icon-circle" style="background:green"></i>';
                            var client_tbody = $('#id_company_status_modal .client-status table tbody').html('');
                            var reseller_tbody = $('#id_company_status_modal .reseller-status table tbody').html('');

                            responsiveTable('#id_company_status_modal');

                            $.each(data,function(ind,val){
                                var status = val.error.length==0?(val.status?st_green:st_red):val.error;
                                if(val.is_reseller){
                                    reseller = true;
                                    $(reseller_tbody).append('<tr><td data-title="SBC">'+val.name+'</td><td data-title="status">'+status+'</td></tr>')
                                    $('.reseller-status').removeClass('hide');
                                }
                                else{
                                    client = true;
                                    $(client_tbody).append('<tr><td data-title="SBC">'+val.name+'</td><td data-title="status">'+status+'</td></tr>')
                                    $('.client-status').removeClass('hide');
                                }
                            });
                            if(data.length==0){
                                $('#id_company_status_modal .alert').removeClass('hide');
                            }
                            else{
                                $('#id_company_status_modal .alert').addClass('hide');
                            }
                            $('#id_company_status_modal .loader').addClass('hide');
                            $('#id_company_status_modal .ui.dimmer').addClass('hide');
                        }
                    })

                }
            })
            .bodal('setting', 'closable', false)
            .bodal('show');
        };



        function GetURLParameter(sParam){
            var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1);
            var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&');

            for(var i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++){
                var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
                if(sParameterName[0] == sParam){
                    return sParameterName[1];
                };
            };
        }

        $(function() {
            
            // To apply multipleSelect on select element.
            // 1- Add class "multipleSelectInit" to initialize.
            // 2- Add attr (data-multipleSelect-placeholder="your placeholder") for placeholder title.
            // 3- Add attr (data-multipleSelect-type="single") for single select.

            $('select.multipleSelectInit').each(function() {
                var $this = $(this),
                    type = $this.attr('data-multipleSelect-type'),
                    placeholder = $this.attr('data-multipleSelect-placeholder'),
                    isSingle = false;
                if (type == 'single') {
                    isSingle = true;
                }
                if (!placeholder) {
                    placeholder = 'an Option'
                }
                $this.find('option').each(function() {
                    var value = $(this).val();
                    if (!value) {
                        $(this).text('Select ' + placeholder).addClass('hide').hide();
                    }
                });
                $this.multipleSelect({
                    placeholder: "Select " + placeholder,
                    filter: true,
                    single: isSingle
                })
            });

             $('body').on('change', '.ui.checkbox.fancy input[type="checkbox"]', function() {
                if($(this).is(':checked')) {
                    $(this).parent().addClass('checked')
                }
                else {
                    $(this).parent().removeClass('checked')
                }   
            });

            $('.ui.checkbox.fancy input[type="radio"]').change(function () {
                var radioName = $(this).attr('name')
                if($(this).is(':checked')) {
                    $(this).parent().addClass('checked')
                }
                else {
                    $(this).parent().removeClass('checked')
                }   
                $('[name="'+radioName+'"]').not(this).prop('checked', false).parent().removeClass('checked')
            });

        });

        // Check Required Fields Function --- START
        function checkRequiredFields($selector) {
            $selector.find('.help-block').remove();
            $selector.find('.field.error').removeClass( 'error' );
            $selector.find('.field.required').not('.not-validate').each( function() {
                var $this = $(this),
                    thisVal = $this.find('input, select, textarea').val();
                if( !thisVal ) {
                    $this.addClass( 'error' );
                    $this.append( '<p class="f-right help-block">This field is required.</p>' );
                }
            });
            if ( $selector.find('.field.error').length == 0 ) {
                return true;
            }
            else {
                return false;
            }
        }
        // Check Required Fields Function --- END

    </script>

            var bindDateTimes = function() {
                $(".datetime").each(function () {
                    try
                    {
                        $(this).datetimepicker({
                                    format: "yyyy-mm-dd hh:ii:00",
                                    weekStart: 1,
                                    todayBtn:  1,
                                    autoclose: 1,
                                    startView: 3,
                                    minView: 0,
                                    forceParse: 0,
                                    minuteStep: 5,
                                    todayHighlight: true
                                    });
                    }
                    catch(e){}
                });
            };

            var bindDates = function() {
                $(".date").each(function () {
                    try
                    {
                        $(this).datetimepicker({
                                    format: "yyyy-mm-dd",
                                    weekStart: 1,
                                    todayBtn:  1,
                                    autoclose: 1,
                                    startView: 3,
                                    minView: 2,
                                    forceParse: 0,
                                    minuteStep: 5,
                                    todayHighlight: true
                                    });
                    }
                    catch(e){}
                });
            };
            var bindTimes = function() {
                $(".time").each(function () {
                    try
                    {
                        $(this).datetimepicker({
                                    format: "hh:ii:00",
                                    weekStart: 1,
                                    todayBtn:  1,
                                    autoclose: 1,
                                    todayHighlight: false,
                                    startView: 1,
                                    minView: 0,
                                    forceParse: 0,
                                    minuteStep: 5,
                                    });
                    }
                    catch(e){}
                });
            };

           var bindMultiselect = function () {
            $(".multiselect").multiselect();
           };

            var bindSortselect= function(){
                var selectedOption;
                $('select:not([data-sorting="false"])').each(function(){
                    selectedOption = $(this).children("option").filter(function(index,option){
                        return $(option).prop("selected");
                    });

                    $(this).html($(this).children("option").sort(function (a, b) {
                        if (a.text.toUpperCase() == b.text.toUpperCase()) return 0;
                        if (a.text.toUpperCase() < b.text.toUpperCase()) return -1;
                        if (a.text.toUpperCase() > b.text.toUpperCase()) return 1;
                    }));
                    //Set selected option
                    $(selectedOption).prop("selected", "selected");
                });
            };

            var bindWidgets = function() {
                bindDateTimes();
                bindDates();
                bindTimes();
                bindMultiselect();
                bindSortselect();
            };

         $("#vendor_rates_preference_details" ).hover(function() {
            if(!$(this).find('ul').length){
                $.get('/bsr/get_mbr_products_wise/', function(data) {
                    var data = $.parseJSON(data);
                    var $DynamicLI = '<ul class="dl-submenu">';
                    $.each(data, function( index, value ) {
                       $DynamicLI += '<li class="dropdown"><a tabindex="-1" href="/bsr/mbr_vendor_preferred_rates/' + value[0] +'">'+ value[1] + '</a></li>';
                    });
                    $DynamicLI += '</ul>'
                    $("#vendor_rates_preference_details" ).append($DynamicLI);
                 });
            }

          }, function() {
